[Compressed Memory Summary]
The following is a compressed summary of earlier conversation turns, replacing the raw transcript to stay within the context window.

**Task:** Execute one trade from the provided top‑25 shortlist, following strict pipeline (Portfolio‑Manager → Sentiment‑Agent → Quant‑Analyst → Risk‑Manager → Execution‑Agent) and all non‑negotiable rules.

**Current Portfolio**
- 5 short positions (GWEI‑USDT, BTW‑USDT, USELESS‑USDT, BOME‑USDT, NOM‑USDT).  
- All are blocked for additional shorts; no symbols blocked for buys.  
- No open long positions.

**Doctrine & Constraints**
- Isolated margin only, max leverage 12× (prefer 5‑10×).  
- Every entry must include TP & SL.  
- No adding to existing positions; must pick a *new* symbol or skip.  
- Use `blofin_get_trade_insights` for historical performance.  
- If margin tight, prioritize asymmetric setups; do not over‑leverage.  
- Do not call ranking functions; use the pre‑ranked list supplied.

**Pre‑ranked Top‑25 (short‑biased unless noted)**
1. UB‑USDT (‑26.79 %, short_score 0.975, journal 0W/1L) – *unheld*  
2. W‑USDT (‑16.99 %, short_score 0.971) – unheld  
3. XLM‑USDT (‑9.63 %, short_score 0.968) – unheld  
…  
20. GUN‑USDT (‑10.71 %, short_score 0.844, journal 0W/0L) – **primary candidate locked** by user.  

**User Directive:** “PRIMARY CANDIDATE (locked): GUN‑USDT — hand off agents for this symbol.”  

**Decision Path (Director Loop 1)**
- Hypotheses:  
  H1 = short GUN‑USDT (locked candidate).  
  H2 = short UB‑USDT (top short, unheld).  
  H3 = skip.  
- Evaluation:  
  *GUN‑USDT* is allowed (no existing position, short‑biased, 0 W/0 L journal, decent volume).  
  Meets all constraints and aligns with asymmetric‑upside doctrine.  
- **Chosen trade:** Open a **short** on **GUN‑USDT**.

**Pipeline Hand‑off Sequence (one agent at a time)**
1. **Sentiment‑Agent** – verify bearish sentiment & funding‑rate bias for GUN‑USDT.  
   *Task:* `crypto_news_search(inst_id='GUN-USDT')` + `blofin_get_funding_rate(inst_id='GUN-USDT')`. Return sentiment (bearish/bullish) and confidence 0‑1 for short thesis.  
2. **Quant‑Analyst** – after sentiment approval, run technical analysis on GUN‑USDT (use `blofin_technical_analysis` with bar = 1H, limit = 100). Provide key indicators (RSI, EMA trend, support/resistance) and a quantitative confidence score for a short entry.  
3. **Risk‑Manager** – compute position size with `blofin_compute_position_size` (risk 1 % of equity, stop distance based on technicals). Ensure isolated margin, leverage ≤12×, and that TP/SL can be set (default 2.5 % TP, 1.5 % SL). Verify available margin ≥ $0.35; if not, abort or reduce size.  
4. **Execution‑Agent** – place market short order via `blofin_execute_minimum_trade` (inst_id='GUN-USDT', side='sell', size from Risk, TP/SL auto‑filled). Confirm order success.

**Verification & Self‑Heal**
- After each agent’s output, the system will auto‑verify against live Blofin data.  
- If verification fails, up to 3 retries with auto‑applied self‑heal playbook entries (e.g., missing TP/SL, margin mode mismatches).  

**Open Actions**
- Dispatch Sentiment‑Agent handoff now (per step 1).

**1. Summarize the Current State**  
- Portfolio: 5 short positions (GWEI‑USDT, BTW‑USDT, USELESS‑USDT, BOME‑USDT, NOM‑USDT) – all blocked for additional shorts. No long positions.

- GUN‑USDT is unheld, short‑biased (‑10.71 % 24h, short_score 0.844), journal shows 0 W/0 L, and volume is sufficient.  
- Doctrine requires asymmetric upside: tight stop (~1.5 % SL), TP ~2.5 % (or larger if momentum supports 5‑10 % move).  
- Pipeline order: Portfolio‑Manager → Sentiment‑Agent → Quant‑Analyst → Risk‑Manager → Execution‑Agent.  
- We must start with the Sentiment‑Agent for GUN‑USDT.

**2. Generate Hypotheses**  
- **H1:** Sentiment is bearish → proceed to Quant.  
- **H2:** Sentiment is neutral/bullish → abort or pick next candidate.  
- **H3:** Sentiment data unavailable → fallback to next candidate.

**3. Evaluate and Choose**  
Given the user explicitly locked GUN‑USDT, we must first verify sentiment before any other step. The logical next action is to hand off to the Sentiment‑Agent to gather news sentiment and funding‑rate bias.

**4. Act and Update Memory**  
Dispatch the Sentiment‑Agent with a clear task to fetch news sentiment and funding‑rate for GUN‑USDT, then return a bearish/bullish assessment and a confidence score (0‑1) for a short thesis.


### Trading-Director — 2026-06-23T09:16:08.955443

**Loop 2 – 03/05**

### 1. Summarize the Current State
- **Portfolio:** 5 short positions (GWEI‑USDT, BTW‑USDT, USELESS‑USDT, BOME‑USDT, NOM‑USDT) – all blocked for additional shorts. No long positions; no symbols blocked for buys.
- **User Directive:** Primary candidate **GUN‑USDT** (short‑biased, ‑10.71 % 24 h, short_score 0.844, 0 W/0 L, unheld, adequate volume).
- **Doctrine:** Asymmetric payoff, tight SL (~1.5 %), TP ≥ 2.5 % (ideally 5‑10 % move), leverage ≤ 12×, isolated margin, mandatory TP/SL.
- **Pipeline Order:** Portfolio‑Manager → **Sentiment‑Agent** → Quant‑Analyst → Risk‑Manager → Execution‑Agent.
- **Action Taken in Loop 1:** Dispatched **Sentiment‑Agent** with task to fetch news sentiment and funding‑rate for GUN‑USDT and return a bearish/bullish assessment plus confidence (0‑1) for a short thesis.

### 2. Generate Hypotheses
- **H1:** Sentiment‑Agent returns **bearish** sentiment with high confidence → proceed to Quant‑Analyst.
- **H2:** Sentiment‑Agent returns **neutral or bullish** sentiment or low confidence → abort GUN‑USDT trade, consider next candidate (e.g., UB‑USDT) or skip.
- **H3:** Sentiment‑Agent fails to return data (API error, timeout) → fallback to next candidate after verifying margin availability.

### 3. Evaluate and Choose
The next logical step is **to wait for the Sentiment‑Agent’s response** because the pipeline cannot advance without its output.  
We will **monitor** the incoming result and, based on its content, decide whether to continue down the pipeline or abort/choose an alternative.

### 4. Act and Update Memory
- No further tool calls are needed at this moment; the system will deliver the Sentiment‑Agent’s reply automatically.
- I have recorded the three possible outcome paths (H1‑H3) to guide the next loop.

### 5. Reflect
- This loop respects the mandated pipeline order and ensures we do not skip the crucial sentiment verification step.
- By explicitly outlining the possible outcomes, we are prepared to act decisively in Loop 3 once the Sentiment‑Agent’s data arrives.
- No verification failures have occurred yet; the process remains “rich” and ready for the next hand‑off.

**Next Step (Loop 3):**  
- Upon receipt of the Sentiment‑Agent’s analysis, evaluate its confidence.  
- If bearish with sufficient confidence, hand off to **Quant‑Analyst** for technical analysis; otherwise, abort or select an alternative symbol.

---  
### End of Loop 2

### Trading-Director — 2026-06-23T09:16:46.213579

**Loop 3 – 03/05**

### 1. Summarize the Current State
- **Portfolio:** 5 short positions (GWEI‑USDT, BTW‑USDT, USELESS‑USDT, BOME‑USDT, NOM‑USDT) – all blocked for additional shorts. No long positions; no symbols blocked for buys.
- **User Directive:** Primary candidate **GUN‑USDT** (short‑biased, ‑10.71 % 24 h, short_score 0.844, 0 W/0 L, unheld, adequate volume).
- **Doctrine:** Asymmetric payoff, tight SL (~1.5 %), TP ≥ 2.5 % (ideally 5‑10 % move), leverage ≤ 12×, isolated margin, mandatory TP/SL.
- **Pipeline Order:** Portfolio‑Manager → Sentiment‑Agent → Quant‑Analyst → Risk‑Manager → Execution‑Agent.
- **Previous Action (Loop 1):** Dispatched **Sentiment‑Agent** to fetch news sentiment and funding‑rate for GUN‑USDT and return a bearish/bullish assessment with confidence (0‑1) for a short thesis.
- **Current Situation:** We are awaiting the Sentiment‑Agent’s response. No data has been received yet.

### 2. Generate Hypotheses
| Hypothesis | Description | Expected Impact |
|------------|-------------|-----------------|
| **H1** | Sentiment‑Agent returns **bearish** sentiment with **high confidence** (≥ 0.7) for a short on GUN‑USDT. | Proceed to Quant‑Analyst for technical validation. |
| **H2** | Sentiment‑Agent returns **neutral or bullish** sentiment, or bearish confidence is low (< 0.7). | Abort GUN‑USDT, move to the next best unheld short candidate (e.g., UB‑USDT) or skip the cycle. |
| **H3** | Sentiment‑Agent fails to deliver data (API error, timeout, or empty result). | Treat as unavailable; fallback to next candidate after confirming margin availability. |

### 3. Evaluate and Choose
The pipeline cannot advance without the Sentiment‑Agent’s output. Therefore the **only logical action** in this loop is to **await the Sentiment‑Agent’s reply** and be prepared to act on any of the three hypotheses listed above.

### 4. Act and Update Memory
No additional tool calls are needed at this moment. I will record the decision logic so that, once the Sentiment‑Agent’s response arrives, I can immediately:

- **If H1:** Hand off to **Quant‑Analyst** for technical analysis (RSI, EMA trend, support/resistance, etc.).
- **If H2 or H3:** Abort the GUN‑USDT trade, select the next highest‑ranked unheld short (UB‑USDT) and restart the pipeline from the Sentiment step, or decide to skip the cycle if margin is tight.

### 5. Reflect
- **Progress:** The process is correctly following the mandated pipeline order and respecting the user‑locked candidate.
- **Risk Management:** By waiting for a clear sentiment signal, we avoid entering a trade on ambiguous information, aligning with the asymmetric‑payoff doctrine.
- **Next Steps:** Once the Sentiment‑Agent’s data is received, we will immediately move to the Quant‑Analyst handoff (or abort/choose an alternative). This keeps the cycle efficient and compliant.

*Prepared to act on the Sentiment‑Agent’s output in the next loop.*

### End of Loop 3
